				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_code et_pb_code_1">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_code_inner"><iframe title="Stella Young Statue Map" src="https://snazzymaps.com/embed/460524" width="100%" height="400px" style="border:none;"></iframe></div>

			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div>
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_4 et_animated et_pb_section_parallax et_pb_with_background et_section_regular" >
				
				<span class="et_parallax_bg_wrap"><span
						class="et_parallax_bg"
						style="background-image: url(https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/water-colour-dark.jpg);"
					></span></span>
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_7">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4 et_pb_column_11  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_5 et_animated  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_dark">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h2>Stella Young, <br />Comedian, Writer, Activist.</h2>
<p>Born in Stawell 24th February 1982</p>
<p>Died in Melbourne 6th December 2014</p></div>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div>
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_5 et_section_regular" >
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_8">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4 et_pb_column_12  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_9 timeline-circle et_animated et-waypoint">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap has-box-shadow-overlay"><div class="box-shadow-overlay"></div><img decoding="async" src="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/early-life.jpg" alt="Stella as a small child wearing a white lacy dress sitting in a pink velvet arm chair." title="early-life" /></span>
			</div><div id="early-life" class="et_pb_module dipl_fancy_text dipl_fancy_text_0 timeline-heading tabindex-1 et_animated">
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module_inner">
					<div class=dipl_gradient>
				<div class="dipl-text-wrapper">
					<div class="dipl-text-wrapper-inner dipl_gradient_text"></p>
<h3>Early Life</h3>
<p></p>
<p>1982 - 1986</p>
<p></div>
				</div>
			</div>
				</div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_6 et_animated  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>Stella Young is born on the 24th of February 1982 in Stawell to Lynne and Greg Young. Lynne runs a local hairdressing salon and Greg works in the family business as a butcher. Later Greg opens a record store just down the road from Lynne’s hairdressing salon.</p>
<p>Stella spends a lot of time at Lynne’s salon, at first playing in a cot as an infant and later helping around the salon after school and in school holidays answering the phone and doing other odd jobs.</p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_10 et_animated et-waypoint">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap has-box-shadow-overlay"><div class="box-shadow-overlay"></div><img decoding="async" src="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/stella-in-the-salon.jpg" alt="Stella is in what looks to be a purpose built red mobility device. Mum Lynne sits at a table. They are in her hairdressing salon." title="stella-in-the-salon" /></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_7 et_animated  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>Lynne and Greg ignored doctors’ warnings about the risk of having another disabled child and Stella’s sisters Romy and Madi were born in 1985 and 1989</p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_11 et_animated et-waypoint">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap has-box-shadow-overlay"><div class="box-shadow-overlay"></div><img decoding="async" width="474" height="394" src="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/Outlook-o5xsgdpm.png" alt="Stella and her two sisters laying in a bed with yellow sheets and pillows" title="Outlook-o5xsgdpm" srcset="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/Outlook-o5xsgdpm.png 474w, https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/Outlook-o5xsgdpm-300x249.png 300w" sizes="(max-width: 474px) 100vw, 474px" class="wp-image-72229" /></span>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div>
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_6 et_section_regular" >
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_row et_pb_row_9 extend-from-left et_animated et_pb_section_parallax">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4 et_pb_column_13  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_blurb et_pb_blurb_1 quote-blurb  et_pb_text_align_left  et_pb_blurb_position_left et_pb_bg_layout_dark">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_blurb_content">
					<div class="et_pb_main_blurb_image"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap et_pb_only_image_mode_wrap"><img decoding="async" src="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/quotes-1.svg" alt="" class="et-waypoint et_pb_animation_top et_pb_animation_top_tablet et_pb_animation_top_phone" /></span></div>
					<div class="et_pb_blurb_container">
						
						<div class="et_pb_blurb_description"><blockquote>
<p>My parents didn&#8217;t know what to do with me so they just pretended I was normal and that worked out quite well for me</p>
</blockquote></div>
					</div>
				</div>
			</div>
			</div>
				<span class="et_parallax_bg_wrap"><span
						class="et_parallax_bg"
						style="background-image: url(https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/water-colour-dark.jpg);"
					></span></span>
				
				
				
			</div>
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_7 et_section_regular" >
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_row et_pb_row_10">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4 et_pb_column_14  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_8 et_animated  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h4>Excerpt from &#8220;A letter to my younger self&#8221;</h4></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_9 et_animated  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><blockquote>
<p>Able-bodiedness is not the Holy Grail. The body that you&#8217;re in is perfectly fine, perfectly beautiful. In fact, you know that thought that sometimes occurs to you — that you&#8217;re actually luckier than the other girls because your body is just too different to compare it to the models in Dolly? That&#8217;s the thought you should indulge.</p>
</blockquote></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module dipl_button dipl_button_0 external-link et_animated">
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module_inner">
					<div class="et_pb_module dipl_button_item dipl_button_item_0">
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module_inner">
					<div class="dipl_button_wrapper dipl_button_classic"><a class="dipl_button_link dipl_button_default_fill" href="https://stellayoung.com.au/a-letter-to-my-younger-self/" target="_self"><span class="dipl_button_text">Read the full letter</span></a></div>
				</div>
			</div>
				</div>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div>
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_8 et_section_regular" >
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_11 gallery-row et_pb_equal_columns et_pb_gutters2">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_3 et_pb_column_15  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_12 gallery-image et_animated et-waypoint">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img decoding="async" src="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/IMG_1014.jpg" alt="Teenage Stella sits on the edge of a pool with wet hair. Her sister Romy stands in the pool with her arms around Stella. Her other sister Madi smiles at the camera from in the pool." title="IMG_1014" /></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_13 gallery-image et_animated et-waypoint">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img decoding="async" src="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/shops-sml.jpg" alt="9 year old Stella poses with her sisters Madi and Romy. They are all wearing primary school uniforms and are gathered outside a shop." title="shops sml" /></span>
			</div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_3 et_pb_column_16  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_14 gallery-image et_animated et-waypoint">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img decoding="async" src="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/Stella-and-her-sisters-2.jpg" alt="8 year old Stella is with her sister Romy and an older girl - possibly a cousin in a suburban street ." title="Stella and her sisters (2)" /></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_15 gallery-image et_animated et-waypoint">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img decoding="async" src="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/Stella-and-her-mum.jpg" alt="Stella and her mother snuggle cheek to cheek, holding lolly pops. They are outdoors in a park." title="Stella-and-her-mum" /></span>
			</div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_3 et_pb_column_17  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_16 gallery-image et_animated et-waypoint">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img decoding="async" src="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/IMG_1027.jpg" alt="4 year old Stella sits in her electric wheelchair while her sister touches the chair&#039;s joystick. They are in a park next to a black swan pecking at the ground." title="IMG_1027" /></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_17 gallery-image et_animated et-waypoint">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img decoding="async" src="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/IMG_0974.jpg" alt="2 year old Stella lovingly cradles her new baby sister who is wearing a hospital tag on her wrist." title="IMG_0974" /></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_18 gallery-image et_animated et-waypoint">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img decoding="async" src="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/Stella-and-her-sisters-0880.jpg" alt="Stella and her two sisters snuggle and smile for the camera on a couch." title="Stella-and-her-sisters---0880" /></span>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div>
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_9 et_section_regular" >
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_12">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4 et_pb_column_18  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_19 timeline-circle et_animated et-waypoint">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap has-box-shadow-overlay"><div class="box-shadow-overlay"></div><img decoding="async" src="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/stella-leaving-homejpg.jpg" alt="Stella in a black dress and short hair" title="stella-leaving-homejpg" /></span>
			</div><div id="leaving-home" class="et_pb_module dipl_fancy_text dipl_fancy_text_1 timeline-heading tabindex-1 et_animated">
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module_inner">
					<div class=dipl_gradient>
				<div class="dipl-text-wrapper">
					<div class="dipl-text-wrapper-inner dipl_gradient_text"></p>
<h3>Leaving Home</h3>
<p></p>
<p>1999 - 2003</p>
<p></div>
				</div>
			</div>
				</div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_10 et_animated  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>In 1999 Stella was accepted into Deakin University in Geelong to study for her bachelor of Arts in Journalism and Public Relations. She later completed a Graduate Diploma in Education at the University of Melbourne.</p>
<p>Stella had learned all about getting around in Melbourne from her friend Caroline Bowditch. Caroline taught her how to catch a train, how to modify her bathroom and a whole lot of other tips that would help Stella live independently in the big city.</p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_20 et_animated et-waypoint">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap has-box-shadow-overlay"><div class="box-shadow-overlay"></div><img decoding="async" src="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/caroline.jpg" alt="Stella with her friend Caroline sitting at a table at home with an open door in the background." title="caroline" /></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_11 et_animated  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>Once settled in Melbourne, Stella became active in the disability community in a variety of roles, including membership of the Victorian Disability Advisory Council, Ministerial Advisory Council for the Department of Victorian communities and Women With Disabilities Victoria.</p>
<p>With a strong interest in issues facing women and young people with disabilities, Stella worked with the Youth Disability Advocacy Service to establish the LiveAccess project, advocating for better access to live music venues.</p></div>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div>
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_10 et_section_regular" >
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_row et_pb_row_13 extend-from-right et_animated et_pb_section_parallax">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4 et_pb_column_19  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_blurb et_pb_blurb_2 quote-blurb  et_pb_text_align_left  et_pb_blurb_position_left et_pb_bg_layout_dark">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_blurb_content">
					<div class="et_pb_main_blurb_image"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap et_pb_only_image_mode_wrap"><img decoding="async" src="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/quotes-1.svg" alt="" class="et-waypoint et_pb_animation_top et_pb_animation_top_tablet et_pb_animation_top_phone" /></span></div>
					<div class="et_pb_blurb_container">
						
						<div class="et_pb_blurb_description"><blockquote>
<p>I started calling myself a disabled woman, and a crip. A good 13 years after 17-year-old me started saying crip, it still horrifies people.</p>
<p>I do it because it&#8217;s a word that makes me feel strong and powerful. It&#8217;s a word other activists have used before me, and I use it to honour them.</p>
</blockquote></div>
					</div>
				</div>
			</div>
			</div>
				<span class="et_parallax_bg_wrap"><span
						class="et_parallax_bg"
						style="background-image: url(https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/water-colour-dark.jpg);"
					></span></span>
				
				
				
			</div>

Stella sits on the rim of the fountain. Her chair is just visible at the edge of the photo." title="stella-water-feature" /></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_22 gallery-image et_animated et-waypoint">

			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_27 gallery-image et_animated et-waypoint">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img decoding="async" src="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/visiting-statue.jpg" alt="Stella and George both in electric wheelchairs pose next to a full height bronze statue of the Queen in a courtyard." title="visiting-statue" /></span>
			</div>

			</div><div class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_12 et_section_regular" >
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_15">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4 et_pb_column_23  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_28 timeline-circle et_animated et-waypoint">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap has-box-shadow-overlay"><div class="box-shadow-overlay"></div><img decoding="async" src="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/community-television.jpg" alt="Stella and other cast on TV" title="community-television" /></span>
			</div><div id="community-television" class="et_pb_module dipl_fancy_text dipl_fancy_text_2 timeline-heading tabindex-1 et_animated">
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module_inner">
					<div class=dipl_gradient>
				<div class="dipl-text-wrapper">
					<div class="dipl-text-wrapper-inner dipl_gradient_text"></p>
<h3>Community Television</h3>
<p></p>
<p>2003 - 2009</p>
<p></div>
				</div>
			</div>
				</div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_12 et_animated  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>Stella was also involved in community television which laid the foundations for her later success in media and comedy.<br />In 2003 Stella joined the community television show “No Limits” as one of the founding presenters.</p>
<p>No Limits brings you unexpected stories about what it’s like living with disability. Presented and produced with disabled people as a place to build community and identity.</p></div>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div>
				
				
			</div><div id="no-limits" class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_13 et_pb_section_parallax et_pb_with_background et_section_regular" >
				
				<span class="et_parallax_bg_wrap"><span
						class="et_parallax_bg"
						style="background-image: url(https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/buildings-bg.jpg);"
					></span></span>
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_16">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4 et_pb_column_24  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_29 no-limits-polygon aria-hidden et_animated et-waypoint">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img decoding="async" src="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/no-limits-shape.png" alt="" title="no-limits-shape" /></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_13 et_animated  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h2><img decoding="async" width="300" height="79" src="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/No-Limits-ident-rough-300x79.png" style="width: 100%; height: auto;" alt="No Limits" class="wp-image-71440 alignnone size-medium" srcset="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/No-Limits-ident-rough-300x79.png 300w, https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/No-Limits-ident-rough-768x203.png 768w, https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/No-Limits-ident-rough-500x132.png 500w, https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/No-Limits-ident-rough-800x211.png 800w, https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/No-Limits-ident-rough-980x259.png 980w, https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/No-Limits-ident-rough-480x127.png 480w, https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/No-Limits-ident-rough.png 1000w" sizes="(max-width: 300px) 100vw, 300px" /></h2></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_code et_pb_code_2">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_code_inner"><video title="No Limits Showreel" class="plyr" playsinline controls data-poster="//cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/no-limits-thumbnail.jpg">

			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_divider_1 no-limits-spacer et_pb_space et_pb_divider_hidden"><div class="et_pb_divider_internal"></div></div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div><div id="camera-rocket-row" class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_17 et_pb_equal_columns">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_2 et_pb_column_25  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_30 et_animated et-waypoint et_pb_image_sticky">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img decoding="async" src="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/video-camera-tall-1.png" alt="Video Camera" title="video-camera-tall" /></span>
			</div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_1_2 et_pb_column_26  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_31 et_animated et-waypoint">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img decoding="async" src="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/no-limits-rocket.png" alt="No Limits Rocket Graphic" title="no-limits-rocket" /></span>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div>
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_14 et_section_regular" >
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_18">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4 et_pb_column_27  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_14 et_animated  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>In 2005 having not been able to get a job as a school teacher, despite many job interviews and great qualifications, Stella begins working at Arts Access Victoria.</p>
<p>She saw working in a disability organisation as a step into the workforce but always hoped to work outside the disability sector.</p>
<p>In 2007 Stella went to work in Public Programs at Melbourne Museum, where she taught kids about bugs, dinosaurs and other weird and wonderful things.</p>
<p>While working at the Museum Stella decided to try her hand a stand-up comedy and was a two-time state finalist in the Melbourne International Comedy Festival’s Raw Comedy competition.</p></div>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div>
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_15 et_section_regular" >

			</div><div class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_16 et_pb_with_background et_section_regular" >
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_20">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_3_5 et_pb_column_31  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_blurb et_pb_blurb_3 quote-blurb et_animated  et_pb_text_align_left  et_pb_blurb_position_left et_pb_bg_layout_dark">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_blurb_content">
					<div class="et_pb_main_blurb_image"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap et_pb_only_image_mode_wrap"><img decoding="async" src="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/quotes-1.svg" alt="" class="et-waypoint et_pb_animation_top et_pb_animation_top_tablet et_pb_animation_top_phone" /></span></div>
					<div class="et_pb_blurb_container">
						
						<div class="et_pb_blurb_description"><blockquote>
<p>I have beautiful interactions with children. I have a responsibility to engage well with children so they don&#8217;t grow up afraid.</p>
<p>One boy asked me, &#8216;Are you imaginary?&#8217; I thought, &#8216;How great he sees magic in this’</p>
<p>If everyone&#8217;s looking at me, I might as well say something interesting.</p>
</blockquote></div>

				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4 et_pb_column_33  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_38 timeline-circle et_animated et-waypoint">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap has-box-shadow-overlay"><div class="box-shadow-overlay"></div><img decoding="async" src="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/ramp-up-and-abcv.jpg" alt="Stella in her wheelchair posing for the camera" title="ramp-up-and-abcv" /></span>
			</div><div id="ramp-up-and-abc" class="et_pb_module dipl_fancy_text dipl_fancy_text_3 timeline-heading tabindex-1 et_animated">
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module_inner">
					<div class=dipl_gradient>
				<div class="dipl-text-wrapper">
					<div class="dipl-text-wrapper-inner dipl_gradient_text"></p>
<h3>Ramp Up and the ABC</h3>
<p></p>
<p>2010 - 2013</p>
<p></div>
				</div>
			</div>
				</div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_15 et_animated  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>In 2010 the Australian Government wanted to elevate discussion around disability ahead of the implementation of the National Disability Insurance Scheme (NDIS).</p>
<p>They awarded funding for this purpose to the Australian Broadcasting Corporation and the disability focused online portal, Ramp Up was established.</p>
<p>Stella Young became its first and only editor.</p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_39 et_animated et-waypoint">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img decoding="async" src="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/ramp-up-logo.jpg" alt="Ramp Up Website Logo with tagline: Disability. Discussion. Debate" title="ramp-up-logo" /></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_16 et_animated  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>Ramp up gave many disabled people the opportunity to write and be published and Stella herself wrote many articles on the issues of the day.</p>
<p>When funding ended for Ramp Up the disability community was dismayed when the ABC announced it would not continue with the site. Stella was deeply disappointed that her community had lost its dedicated space at the national broadcaster but on a personal level Stella was now free to pursue the many offers she was receiving.</p></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module dipl_button dipl_button_1 external-link et_animated">
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module_inner">
					<div class="et_pb_module dipl_button_item dipl_button_item_1">
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module_inner">
					<div class="dipl_button_wrapper dipl_button_conversion"><a class="dipl_button_link dipl_button_default_fill" href="https://www.abc.net.au/rampup/" target="_self"><span class="dipl_button_text">Read Stella&#039;s Articles</span><span class="dipl_button_secondary_text">(external link)</span></a></div>
				</div>
			</div>
				</div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_17 et_animated  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>In 2012 Stella became engaged to her long term partner. The engagement didn’t bring her the joy she had hoped for and after careful consideration she ended the engagement and the relationship a few months later.</p>
<p>As a newly single woman she moved into her own pad in Melbourne’s ritzy South Yarra and barely spent an evening at home.  Life was full, hectic and fun.</p></div>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div>
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_18 et_section_regular" >

Stella&#039;s red spotted shoes are just visible and a star brooch is pinned to her top." title="governor" /></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_41 gallery-image et_animated et-waypoint">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img decoding="async" src="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/knuckles-sml.jpg" alt="Stella is one of four smiling women holding up their knuckles in a row. 			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_43 gallery-image et_animated et-waypoint">

			</div>

			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div>
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_19 et_section_regular" >
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_23">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4 et_pb_column_38  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_18 et_animated  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>Alongside multiple appearances on the ABC, SBS and Channel 10’s The Project, Stella began working on a solo show for the Melbourne International comedy Festival.</p>
<p>2014 was a huge year for Stella. It was also her last. </p></div>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div>

			</div><div id="ted-talk" class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_23 et_section_regular" >
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_31">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4 et_pb_column_54  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_image et_pb_image_60 et_animated et-waypoint">
				
				
				
				
				<span class="et_pb_image_wrap "><img decoding="async" src="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/TED_wordmark.svg.png" alt="TED Ideas worth spreading logo" title="TED_wordmark.svg" /></span>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_19 et_animated  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><h2>I&#8217;m Not Your Inspiration, Thank You Very Much</h2></div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_code et_pb_code_3">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_code_inner"><div class="plyr" data-plyr-provider="youtube" data-plyr-embed-id="8K9Gg164Bsw" data-plyr-config='{ "title": "Stellas Ted Talk" }'></div></div>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_row et_pb_row_32">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4 et_pb_column_55  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_20 et_animated  et_pb_text_align_center et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>In April she presented her now famous TED talk in Sydney, where she introduced the idea of Inspiration porn and explained to the world why she didn’t want to be anyone’s inspiration.</p></div>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div>
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_24 et_section_regular" >
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_with_border et_pb_row et_pb_row_33 extend-from-left et_animated et_pb_section_parallax">
				<div class="et_pb_column et_pb_column_4_4 et_pb_column_56  et_pb_css_mix_blend_mode_passthrough et-last-child">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module et_pb_blurb et_pb_blurb_4 quote-blurb  et_pb_text_align_left  et_pb_blurb_position_left et_pb_bg_layout_dark">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_blurb_content">
					<div class="et_pb_main_blurb_image"><span class="et_pb_image_wrap et_pb_only_image_mode_wrap"><img decoding="async" src="https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/quotes-1.svg" alt="" class="et-waypoint et_pb_animation_top et_pb_animation_top_tablet et_pb_animation_top_phone" /></span></div>
					<div class="et_pb_blurb_container">
						
						<div class="et_pb_blurb_description"><blockquote>
<p>Let me be clear about the intent of this inspiration porn; it&#8217;s there so that non-disabled people can put their worries into perspective.</p>
<p>So they can go, &#8220;Oh well if that kid who doesn&#8217;t have any legs can smile while he&#8217;s having an awesome time, I should never, EVER feel bad about my life&#8221;.</p>
<p>It&#8217;s there so that non-disabled people can look at us and think &#8220;well, it could be worse&#8230; I could be that person”&#8230;</p>
</blockquote></div>
					</div>
				</div>
			</div>
			</div>
				<span class="et_parallax_bg_wrap"><span
						class="et_parallax_bg"
						style="background-image: url(https://cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/uploads/2023/03/water-colour-dark.jpg);"
					></span></span>
				
				
				
			</div>
				
				
			</div><div class="et_pb_section et_pb_section_25 et_section_regular" >

She&#039;s holding a full glass of beer." title="inspiration" /></span>
			</div><div id="visiting-the-us" class="et_pb_module dipl_fancy_text dipl_fancy_text_4 timeline-heading tabindex-1 et_animated">
				
				
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_module_inner">
					<div class=dipl_gradient>
				<div class="dipl-text-wrapper">
					<div class="dipl-text-wrapper-inner dipl_gradient_text"></p>
<h3>Visiting the United States</h3>
<p></p>
<p>2014</p>
<p></div>
				</div>
			</div>
				</div>
			</div><div class="et_pb_module et_pb_text et_pb_text_21 et_animated  et_pb_text_align_left et_pb_bg_layout_light">
				
				
				
				
				<div class="et_pb_text_inner"><p>In July Stella travelled to the United States on a Cultural Vistas Fellowship.</p>
<p>Highlights included a visit to the US State Department and a meeting with disability rights pioneer and Special Advisor on International Disability Rights Judy Heumann, a visit to the set of Sesame Street and meetings with an array of US disability rights campaigners and activists.</p></div>
			</div>
			</div>
				
				
				
				
			</div>

<script type="text/javascript">
	(function($) {
		
		// Add negative tabindexes to elements with class .tabindex-1
		let tabIndexes = document.querySelectorAll('.tabindex-1');
		for (var i = 0; i < tabIndexes.length; i++) {
			tabIndexes[i].setAttribute('tabindex', '-1');
		}
						
		// Missing Aria landmarks
		let mainNavs = document.querySelectorAll('.primary-menu nav');
		for(var i = 0; i < mainNavs.length; i++) {
			mainNavs[i].setAttribute('aria-label', 'Main');
		}
		
		let secondaryNavs = document.querySelectorAll('.hero-nav nav');
		for(var i = 0; i < secondaryNavs.length; i++) {
			secondaryNavs[i].setAttribute('aria-label', 'Page');
		}
		
		// Add aria-hidden="true" to any elements with class aria-hidden
		let hidden = document.querySelectorAll('.aria-hidden');
		for(var i = 0; i < hidden.length; i++) {
			hidden[i].setAttribute('aria-hidden', true);
		}
		
		// Scroll to top button
		let stt = document.querySelectorAll('.et_pb_scroll_top');
		for(var i = 0; i < stt.length; i++) {
			stt[i].setAttribute('aria-role', 'button');
			stt[i].setAttribute('aria-label', 'Scroll back to top');
		}
		
		// On page load focus on the anchor in the URL if exists
		let hash = window.location.hash.substr(1);
		if(hash) {
			setFocusOnID(hash);
		}
		
		// Change browser focus after clicking an anchor link (for screen readers)
		document.querySelectorAll('a[href^="/#"]').forEach(anchor => {
			addClickFocusEventListener(anchor);
		});
		document.querySelectorAll('a[href^="#"]').forEach(anchor => {
			addClickFocusEventListener(anchor);
		});
				
		function addClickFocusEventListener(anchor) {			
			anchor.addEventListener('click', function (e) {
				//e.preventDefault();
				let id = this.getAttribute('href').split('#')[1]
				setFocusOnID(id);
			});
		}
		
		function setFocusOnID(id) {
			let target = document.getElementById(id);
			if(target != null) {
				target.focus();
			}
		}
		
		// Plyr.io set up
		const players = Array.from(document.querySelectorAll('.plyr')).map((p) => {
			new Plyr(p, {
				iconUrl: '//cdn10427.templcdn.com/wp-content/themes/stellayoung/includes/sprite/plyr-custom.svg',
				controls: [
					//'play-large', 
					'play', 
					'rewind',
					'fast-forward',
					'progress', 
					'current-time', 
					'mute', 
					'volume', 
					'captions', 
					'settings', 
					//'pip', 
					//'airplay', 
					'fullscreen'
				],
				i18n: {
					rewind: 'skip backward 10 seconds',
					fastForward: 'skip forward 10 seconds'
				}
			});
		});
	})(jQuery);
